<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-sections-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#sections-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Sections <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="books" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f4da.png">📚</g-emoji></h1>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Summary and About me<br>
<g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Skills <br>
<g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Open Source Projects Connected with Github<br>
<g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Experience<br>
<g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Certifications <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="trophy" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f3c6.png">🏆</g-emoji><br>
<g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Blogs<br>
<g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Education<br>
<g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="heavy_check_mark" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2714.png">✔️</g-emoji> Contact me</p>
<p dir="auto">To view a live example, <strong><a href="https://ashutosh1919.github.io/" rel="nofollow">click here</a></strong></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-clone-and-use-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#clone-and-use-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Clone And Use <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="clipboard" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f4cb.png">📋</g-emoji></h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>The website is completely built on <code>react-js</code> library of <code>javascript</code> and that's why we need <code>nodejs</code> and <code>npm</code> installed.</li>
<li>While installing <code>nodejs</code> and <code>npm</code>, try to install versions which are equal or greater than the versions mentioned in badges above.</li>
<li>In case you want to help developing it or simply saving it, you can fork the repository just by clicking the button on the top-right corner of this page.</li>
<li>After the successful installation of <code>nodejs</code> and <code>npm</code>, clone the repository into your local system using below command:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" git clone https://github.com/ashutosh1919/masterPortfolio.git"><pre> git clone https://github.com/ashutosh1919/masterPortfolio.git</pre></div>
</li>
<li>This will clone the whole repository in your system.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>To download required dependencies to your system, navigate to the directory where the cloned repository resides and execute following command:
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="npm install"><pre><span class="pl-s1">npm</span> <span class="pl-s1">install</span></pre></div>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Now, the project is ready to use.</li>
<li>You can check it using <code>npm start</code>, it will open the website locally on your browser.</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-customize-it-to-make-your-own-portfolio-️" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#customize-it-to-make-your-own-portfolio-️"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Customize it to make your own portfolio <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="pencil2" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/270f.png">✏️</g-emoji></h1>
<p dir="auto">In this project, there are basically 4 things that you need to change to customize this to anyone else's portfolio: <strong>package.json</strong>, <strong>Personal Information</strong>, <strong>Github Information</strong> and <strong>Splash Logo</strong>.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-packagejson" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#packagejson"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>package.json</h3>
<p dir="auto">Open this file, which is in the main cloned directory, choose any "name" and change "homepage " to <code>https://&lt;your-github-username&gt;.github.io</code>. Do not forget the <code>https://</code>, otherwise fonts will not load.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-personal-information" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#personal-information"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Personal Information</h3>
<p dir="auto">You will find <code>src/portfolio.js</code> file which contains the complete information about the user. The file looks something like below:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Home Page
const greeting = {
    ...
}

// Social Media
const socialMediaLinks = {
    ...
}

..."><pre><span class="pl-c">// Home Page</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">greeting</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    ...
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-c">// Social Media</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">socialMediaLinks</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    ...
<span class="pl-kos">}</span>

<span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can change the personal information, experience, education, social media, certifications, blog information, contact information etc. in <code>src/portfolio.js</code> to directly reflect them in portfolio website.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-github-information" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#github-information"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Github Information</h3>
<p dir="auto">You will find <code>git_data_fetcher.mjs</code> file in the main directory of the repository. This file is used to fetch the data (Pull requests, Issues, Organizations, Pinned projects etc.) from your github.
If you open the file, you will see below component at the top of the file. You need to change only that component.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="const openSource = {
  githubConvertedToken: &quot;Your Github Token Here.&quot;,
  githubUserName: &quot;Your Github Username Here.&quot;,
};"><pre><span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">openSource</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">githubConvertedToken</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Your Github Token Here."</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">githubUserName</span>: <span class="pl-s">"Your Github Username Here."</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">You can get a github token as described <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/authenticating-to-github/creating-a-personal-access-token">here</a>. Give all permissions while generating token. Also add your <code>githubUserName</code> in the correct field inside <code>git_data_fetcher.js</code>.
Now, you need to run following command.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Warning:</strong> Treat your tokens like passwords and keep them secret. When working with the API, use tokens as environment variables instead of hardcoding them into your programs.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="node git_data_fetcher.mjs"><pre><span class="pl-s1">node</span> <span class="pl-s1">git_data_fetcher</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">mjs</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This will fetch all the data from your github and it will automatically replace my data with yours.
Whenever you want to update the github related information on the website you need to run this command.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-splash-logo" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#splash-logo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Splash Logo</h3>
<p dir="auto">Note here that if you click <a href="https://ashutosh1919.github.io" rel="nofollow">my portfolio</a>, you can see animating the logo at the beginning. I have designed that logo in <a href="https://www.figma.com/" rel="nofollow"><code>Figma</code></a> and then animated it using css.
Therefore, this part of portfolio is not customizable. But don't worry we have a solution to this problem. You have below two alternatives:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">If you want to design your own logo, then you can design it using <code>Figma</code> or <code>Adobe XD</code> or <code>Adobe Illustrator</code> or <code>Inkscape</code>. If you want to animate it, you can refer to <code>./src/components/Loader</code> directory which contains <code>js</code> and <code>css</code> files which animates the logo.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">If you don't want Splash screen or you don't know how to design logo, then this option is for you.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>You can open <code>src/portfolio.js</code> file and at the top of this file you will see <code>settings</code> component as below:</li>
<li>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="// Website related settings
const settings = {
  isSplash: false,
};"><pre><span class="pl-c">// Website related settings</span>
<span class="pl-k">const</span> <span class="pl-s1">settings</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">isSplash</span>: <span class="pl-c1">true</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>Change <code>isSplash</code> from <code>true</code> to <code>false</code>.</li>
<li>Now, if you see your website using <code>npm start</code>, it will directly open <code>home</code> rather than animating logo <code>splash</code> screen.</li>
<li>If you design your logo in future, then edit the files in <code>./src/components/Loader</code> and then revert <code>isSplash</code> to <code>true</code> in <code>src/portfolio.js</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-other" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#other"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Other</h2>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">You need to change the website title and other descriptions in <code>public/index.html</code></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">You can define your own favicon in <code>public/icons</code> directory. If you don't have a favicon, you can generate favicons from <a href="https://www.favicon-generator.org/" rel="nofollow">Favicon Generator</a> and <a href="https://favicon.io/" rel="nofollow">Favicon IO</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Also you can edit your website preview known as description image. Run your site locally, take a screenshot and replace with <code>public/icons/desc.png</code>. Note that your screenshot should be 1280x640 for better preview</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-choose-theme-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#choose-theme-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Choose Theme <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="rainbow" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f308.png">🌈</g-emoji></h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">You can take a look at <code>src/theme.js</code> file where all available themes are mentioned with respective color codes.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">At the bottom of this file you will see the below code:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>export const chosenTheme = blueTheme;</code></li>
<li>You need to change the name from <code>blueTheme</code> to whatever theme you want to set your website to.</li>
<li>You can define new theme similarly as other themes and you can assign name of that new defined theme to <code>chosenTheme</code>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">That's it. You just need to change the theme name and the code will take care of everything else.</p>
<p dir="auto">Run <code>npm start</code> to check if everything is ok.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-deployment-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#deployment-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Deployment <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="package" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f4e6.png">📦</g-emoji></h1>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Once you are done with your setup and have successfully completed all steps above, you need to put your website online!</li>
<li>I highly recommend using <a href="https://create-react-app.dev/docs/deployment/#github-pages" rel="nofollow">Github Pages</a> to achieve this the EASIEST WAY.</li>
<li>To deploy your website, you have two options. First you need to create a github repository with the name <code>&lt;your-github-username&gt;.github.io</code>. Please don't give it any other name.</li>
<li>Now, you need to generate a production build and deploy the website.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Option 1:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Run <code>npm run build</code> to generate the production build folder.</li>
<li>Enter the build folder, <code>git init</code> and push the generated code to the <code>master</code> branch of your new repository. That's it. Done.
You may need to <code>git init</code> and force push at every new build.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Option 2 (will not work with <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/working-with-github-pages/about-github-pages">user pages</a>):</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Run <code>npm run deploy</code> to build and create a branch called <code>gh-pages</code>. It will push the <code>build</code> files to that branch.</li>
<li>The last step in deploying is to enable <code>Github Pages</code> in settings of the repository and select <code>gh-pages</code> branch.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Now, your website is successfully deployed and you can visit it at <code>&lt;your-github-username&gt;.github.io</code>.<br>
If you are stuck somewhere and want to observe the deployment process in depth, then please watch below video.</p>
<p align="center" dir="auto"> 
    <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IwBS39TOmpA" rel="nofollow">
    <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/9c5ae31512156e98e519be530c30e4245964ceb386018ab2dc70cc4c67296dc1/687474703a2f2f696d672e796f75747562652e636f6d2f76692f497742533339544f6d70412f302e6a7067" data-canonical-src="http://img.youtube.com/vi/IwBS39TOmpA/0.jpg" style="max-width: 100%;">
  </a>
</p>
